Cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Scots_language" class="extiw" title="w:Scots language">Scots</a></span> <i class="Latn <ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:archaic.html>archaic</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:piece.html>piece</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:forest.html>forest</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a> cleared <a href = vnd.unilang:for.html>for</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:agriculture.html>agriculture</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:habitation.html>habitation</a>; <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> clearing; assart</li></ol>

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a
